				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Das wohltemperierte Klavier I, BWV 846-869 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.25em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:80%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="left"><center>This page is <b>only</b> for <b>complete</b> editions and multiple selections from <i>Das wohltemperierte Klavier I</i>. For most arrangements, see the separate pages<br />for the individual preludes and fugues. For the later set of 24 preludes and fugues, see: <i><a href="/wiki/Das_wohltemperierte_Klavier_II,_BWV_870-893_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Das wohltemperierte Klavier II, BWV 870-893 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Das wohltemperierte Klavier II</a></i>, BWV 870-893.</center></td></tr></table></div>
<div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>24 preludes and fugues
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1722
</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>

<th>Publisher Info.
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://music.ibiblio.org/pub/multimedia/pandora/HOMEPAGE.html">Pandora Records/Al Goldstein Archive</a></span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td><i>Source and alternative formats</i>: <span class="expandline"><br />From an <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ibiblio.org/pandora/mp3/historical_instruments/Flemish_harpsichord/">album featuring a Flemish harpsichord</a></span> on Pandora Records. Ogg Vorbis files can be found <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ibiblio.org/pandora/vorbis/historical_instruments/Flemish_harpsichord/"><b>here</b></a></span>.</span><br /><i>Instrument used</i>: <span class="expandline"><br />The harpsichord is copied from a one manual instrument built by Hans Moerman in Antwerp (1584). It was restored by Frank Hubbard in Boston (1963). The working plans of the instrument used are due to Lutz Bungart of the Instrument workshop. It was built in the the early seventies by <a href="/wiki/Category:Goldstein,_Al" title="Category:Goldstein, Al">Al Goldstein</a> when he was the partner of Lutz. The instrument has 2 manuals in the usual dispostion of 8x8x4.</span>
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Das wohltemperierte Klavier I (The Well-Tempered Clavier)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Praeludia und Fugen durch alle Tone und Semitonia (Preludes and Fugues through all tones and semitones)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="de, nl">Das wohltemperierte Klavier I</span>; <span title="en">The Well-Tempered Clavier 1</span>; <span title="fr">Le Clavier bien tempéré, Livre I</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/301462774">WorldCat</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/301462774">301462774</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n80109808">n80109808</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/30001189X">30001189X</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LIBRIS" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:LIBRIS">SELIBR</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://libris.kb.se/auth/226799">226799</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td>IJB 721
</td></tr>
<tr>

<dl><dd>1. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_C_major,_BWV_846_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in C major, BWV 846 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in C major, BWV 846</a></i>

</dd><dd>2. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_C_minor,_BWV_847_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in C minor, BWV 847 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in C minor, BWV 847</a></i>
<dl><dd>(alternative version: BWV 847a)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>3. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_C-sharp_major,_BWV_848_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in C-sharp major, BWV 848 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in C-sharp major, BWV 848</a></i>
</dd><dd>4. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_C-sharp_minor,_BWV_849_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in C-sharp minor, BWV 849 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in C-sharp minor, BWV 849</a></i>
</dd><dd>5. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_D_major,_BWV_850_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in D major, BWV 850 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in D major, BWV 850</a></i>
<dl><dd>(alternative version: BWV 850a)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>6. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_D_minor,_BWV_851_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in D minor, BWV 851 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in D minor, BWV 851</a></i>
<dl><dd>(alternative version: BWV 851a)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>7. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_E-flat_major,_BWV_852_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in E-flat major, BWV 852 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in E-flat major, BWV 852</a></i>
</dd><dd>8. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_E-flat_minor,_BWV_853_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in E-flat minor, BWV 853 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in E-flat minor, BWV 853</a></i> (the Fugue is in D<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266f;</span> minor)
</dd><dd>9. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_E_major,_BWV_854_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in E major, BWV 854 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in E major, BWV 854</a></i>

<dl><dd>(alternative version: BWV 855a)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>11. <i><a href="/wiki/Prelude_and_Fugue_in_F_major,_BWV_856_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Prelude and Fugue in F major, BWV 856 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Prelude and Fugue in F major, BWV 856</a></i>
